 ___________________________________________________________________
      Noemia Reis
Capoeira at University of Alaska Anchorage taught by Noemia Reis. It
is a university class, so you have to sign up at the beginning of each
semester. There is only one class, so there is a mixture of beginners and
more experienced students in it. It is a three hour, once weekly class.
SOURCE:
http://www.facebook.com/topic.php?uid=164663273543711&topic=221
Noemia currently gives dance classes that include some aspects of capoeira,
but the classes aren't advertised as such.  She has thought about
giving classes that focus solely on capoeira.People here in Anchorage have
expressed interest in learning capoeira, so it may be an option to provide
this.
email 9/3/02
I am thinking about starting a capoeira class here soon.
email 9/9/02

        Grupo Farol da Bahia
Capoeira Teacher Name  Piton
About Me  Salve !!! Meu nome eh Bruna Smith,moro em Anchorage
[Alaska] gostaria de voltar a treinar mas nao encontrei nenhum lugar que
tenha capoeira aqui no Alaska... Comecei a treinar em 1994, quando eu tinha
13 anos,na Academia Farol da Bahia em Curitiba - PR "BRASIL"... fiquei
por + ou - 5 e infelizmente parei... Essa arte que encanta...aiaiai eu
nao queria sair...A bendita capoeira... que veio dos ancestrais...Salve
o mestre Seu Piton... que me ensinou o abc...Deus lhe cuide, Deus lhe ajude,
eu nunca mais vou te esquecer... Mas vou;>>> Vou Girar o mundo...
SOURCE : capoeira com  member Last visited site  Thursday
11 August 2005 - 13:31:21

                       The Capoeira List
      Lancaster

Mon Sep 12 2005, 08:38
This is just to let you know that I have started an informal capoeira
practice group in Lancaster [lancs. england, UK].
The group meets once a week on Fridays. We also plan workshops with
visiting instructors, trips to events etc. Its basically a way for capoeiristas
in the area to keep in touch and practice in the absence of an instructor.
If you're interested get in touch.
mat[underscore]weldon[at]yahoo[dot]co[dot]uk
SOURCE: www.capoeira.com

                       Decorah

(We are gathering a group of individuals who have practiced and or
would like to practice the Afro-Brazilian fighting art of Capoeira. Mestre
Yoji Senna of the Afro-Brazilian Capoeira Association in Minneapolis will
come to Decorah once a month to instruct our group and guide it. We will
hold weekly classes to keep our skills sharp. This art is a beautiful combination
of music, dancing and fighting that is a great way to get in shape, meet
new people, learn new culture, and have fun!)

    in the end of 2002 i heard about capoeira
near my
    house  [in israel] i didnt know 
what it was so i went to check it
     out....it was  AWSOME i
loved it i used to practise with 3 freinds more
     than 3 hours a day  EVERYDAY
i wouldnt/ couldnt miss out on it!! it was
     like a lifestyle to me! 
i have been to 1 batizado and i used to take
     classes with "Batus Capoeira 
[mastre Pintor]"
    i got a yeelow/black belt in the batizado....

                 Gambier

      Kenyon College Capoeira Club
Capoeira Club: The objective of the Kenyon Capoeira Club is to promote
the Brazilian Martial Art/Dance capoeira among the college population This
will be done through member participation in practicing the movements and
learning about the music of the art, as well as through increased self
awareness and confidence in the participants. It offers physical and mental
tools to deal with difficult situations.
SOURCE http://www2.kenyon.edu/depts/multicultural/orgs.htm

                 Denton

      Denton Capoeira
http://www.dogtato.net/capoeira.html
capoeira@dogtato.net
(I practiced Capoeira for several years in College Station and now
I practice alone. If you want someone to practice and play with, or if
you've never done it and want to try, I am free for both. Literally, I'll
teach you for free, since I'm not particularly qualified such that I could
justify charging a fee. If you're better than me, I won't pester you to
teach me but I might about playing.)
(I think the gym area at a rec center like Denia would be a good
place, since you can get access to it for something like $5/yr and there's
plenty of space and it's indoors. When the weather is nice, practicing
outside is fine.)

 ___________________________________________________________________

Master Alfredo Borges, Bahia, Brazil, will lead a workshop in capoeira,
an Afro-Brazilian dance form that incorporates martial arts, acrobatics,
music and dance, from 2 to 4 p.m Saturday [April 23] in Theater Hall Room
132. Borges is a professional dancer who has led workshops in many countries.
Anyone interested in attending the free workshop should sign up by calling
student Fabio De Barros at 360-0892. Borges and other dancers will demonstrate
capoeira Saturday evening during the program at the International Dinner
that starts at 5:30 p.m. in the University Union.
SOURCE: http://www.uwgb.edu/univcomm/news/logarchive/logarchive36/2005apr21.htm

       Brazilian Regional Capoeira
 Classification:  Recreational
 Campus Mail:  Union Box 95
 Contacts:  Claudia Francioli, 332-9662
Harrison Schultz, 482-1025
 E-Mail:  claudia@uwm.edu
 BRC will incorporate the following: physical training, learning
the steps
and dance of capoeira, the music & musical instruments related
to the art
of capoeira, historical and theoretical classes developing on the history
of Brazilian Regional Capoeira.
Activities:  The program will consist of 2 classes per week, one
hour
each, in which the instructor will teach activities related to capoeira
regional. Annually there will be an event in which the group will
demonstrate what has been learned

 ___________________________________________________________________

College of Health Sciences
Department of Human Movement Sciences
Course Title: 928-293 Capoeira
Location: Westminster Presbyterian Church
2308 E Belleview
Instructor: Thomas E. Bartylla
Prerequisites: None
Required Material: None
Course Description/Objectives:
Capoeira Angola is an art of the African Diaspora that originated in
Angola where it was designed to teach its practitioners philosophy, self-protection,
music and meditation. The objective of the first course is to introduce
students to the basic movements, rhythms and philosophy of Capoeira Angola.
To further broaden the scope of the lessons, students will also have readings
that relate to the discussions on particular topics
SOURCE:http://www.uwm.edu/CHS/descriptions/928-293capoeira.html
: September 24, 2002

from instructors that would like to give work shops in capoeira, drumming
